In practice, all consumers within a share group typically subscribe to the same topic or topics.\n378:     <p>\n379:     When a consumer in a share-group fetches records, it receives available records from any of the topic-partitions matching its subscriptions. Records are acquired for delivery to this consumer with a time-limited\n380:     acquisition lock. While a record is acquired, it is unavailable to other consumers.\n381:     <p>By default, the lock duration is 30 seconds, but you can control it using the group configuration parameter <code>share.record.lock.duration.ms</code>. bootstrapServers, String groupId) {\n        this.bootstrapServers = bootstrapServers;\n        this.groupId = groupId;\n        this.closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);\n    }\n\n    public void start() {\n        consumer = createKafkaConsumer();\n        consumer.subscribe(Collections.singletonList(\"inventory-updates\"));\n\n        try {\n            while (!closed.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(1000));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    processMessage(record);\n                }\n                // Commit offsets after processing each batch to ensure idempotent processing\n                consumer.commitSync();\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            // Ignore exception if we are shutting down\n            if (!closed.get()) {\n                throw e;\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Process a single inventory update message idempotently.\n     * This method should be designed to handle duplicate messages gracefully.\n     */\n    private void processMessage(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        // Implementation for processing inventory update\n        // This ensures idempotent processing of messages\n        String key = record.key();\n        String value = record.value();\n\n        // Process the inventory update message\n        // Idempotent processing ensures that processing the same message multiple times\n        // produces the same result as processing it once\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Shutdown the consumer gracefully.\n     * Can be called from a different thread.\n     */\n    public void shutdown() {\n        closed.set(true);\n        if (consumer != null) {\n            consumer.wakeup();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a KafkaConsumer with proper configuration using ConsumerConfig constants.\n     */\n    private KafkaConsumer<String, String> createKafkaConsumer() {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n\n        // Use ConsumerConfig constants for all configuration keys (not string literals)\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, bootstrapServers);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_ID_CONFIG, groupId);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.KEY_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.VALUE_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n\n        // Disable auto-commit to ensure we control when offsets are committed\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG, false);\n\n        // Set auto offset reset to earliest for idempotent processing\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.AUTO_OFFSET_RESET_CONFIG, \"earliest\");\n\n        return new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n    }\n\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        String bootstrapServers = args.length > 0 ? args[0] : \"localhost:9092\";\n        String groupId = args.length > 1 ? args[1] : \"inventory-consumer-group\";\n\n        InventoryConsumer consumer = new InventoryConsumer(bootstrapServers, groupId);\n\n        // Handle shutdown gracefully\n        Runtime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(consumer::shutdown));\n\n        consumer.start();\n
